GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*(c6 - P/c7)*P + c8*(c9 - exp(-c10*P))*P
Candidate formulas: 50

GT depends **only on P** (no t). Expand GT to see its functional form:

\[
\text{GT}(P)=a\Big[(-1+P/\alpha)(1-P/\beta)P+(1-P/\beta)P+(1-e^{-kP})P\Big]
\]
with fixed \(a=0.1699888\), \(\alpha=1.047284367\), \(\beta=10.210545156\), \(k=0.09709294494\).

First two bracketed terms simplify:
\[
(-1+P/\alpha)(1-P/\beta)P+(1-P/\beta)P = (P/\alpha)(1-P/\beta)P = \frac{1}{\alpha}P^2-\frac{1}{\alpha\beta}P^3
\]
So
\[
\text{GT}(P)=a\left(\frac{1}{\alpha}P^2-\frac{1}{\alpha\beta}P^3 + P - P e^{-kP}\right)
\]
This is **polynomial (up to \(P^3\)) plus a non-polynomial term** \(-a\,P e^{-kP}\). Any matching candidate must be able to represent \(P e^{-kP}\) exactly (for all real \(P\)), and must have **no residual t-dependence** after parameter choices.

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

## GT Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.1699888096710614*(-1 + P/1.0472843670254641)*(1 - P/10.210545156320043)*P + 0.1699888096710614*(1 - P/10.210545156320043)*P + 0.1699888096710614*(1 - exp(-0.09709294493863778*P))*P
```

Let me expand this. Let me denote α = 0.16999, a = 1.04728, b = 10.2105, β = 0.09709.

**Term 1:** α*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P
= α*(P/a - 1)*(1 - P/b)*P
= α*P*(P/a - 1)(1 - P/b)
= α*P*[P/a - P²/(ab) - 1 + P/b]
= α*[-P + P²/a - P³/(ab) + P²/b]
= -α*P + α*P²/a + α*P²/b - α*P³/(ab)

**Term 2:** α*(1 - P/b)*P
= α*P - α*P²/b

**Term 3:** α*(1 - exp(-β*P))*P
= α*P - α*P*exp(-β*P)

**Combining all terms:**
- P³ term: -α/(ab)
- P² terms: α/a + α/b - α/b = α/a
- P terms: -α + α + α = α
- Exponential term: -α*P*exp(-β*P)

So GT = **-α/(ab) * P³ + α/a * P² + α * P - α*P*exp(-β*P)**

Numerically:
- P³ coefficient: -0.16999/(1.04728 * 10.2105) ≈ -0.01589
- P² coefficient: 0.16999/1.04728 ≈ 0.16228
- P coefficient: 0.16999
- Exponential term: -0.16999 * P * exp(-0.09709*P)

So GT = c₀*P³ + c₁*P² + c₂*P + c₃*P*exp(c₄*P)

where c₃ = -0.16999 and c₄ = -0.09709.

This has the form: **polynomial in P (cubic) + P*exp(negative*P) term**, and **no dependence on t**.

Now I'll check each candidate against this structure. The GT requires:
1. P³ term
2. P² term  
3. P term
4. P*exp(c*P) term
5. No t dependence
6. No constant term (when P=0, GT=0)

Let me systematically check candidates:

**Candidates that are purely polynomial in P (no exp(P) term):** These cannot match because they lack the P*exp(cP) basis function.

Candidates 1, 9, 10, 13, 14, 15, 16, 20, 21: Pure polynomials in P (possibly with t-dependent or constant terms that could be zeroed). Missing P*exp(cP) → **NO MATCH**

**Candidates with t-dependence that can't be zeroed:**

- Candidate 3: Has P*c₅*exp(c₆*|P|) and exp(c₉*t). Set c₈=0 for t term. With P≥0, |P|=P. So: P³c₀+P²(c₁+c₂+c₃)+P(c₄+c₇)+Pc₅*exp(c₆P). This matches the GT structure! GT=0 at P=0 and no constant → need c₈=0 (already set). **MATCH**

Let me verify Candidate 3 carefully:
P³*c0 + P²*c1 + P²*c2 + P²*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5*exp(c6*|P|) + P*c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)

Set c8=0 (removes t). With P≥0, |P|=P:
= c0*P³ + (c1+c2+c3)*P² + (c4+c7)*P + c5*P*exp(c6*P)
